Opening of the Capital Construction Conference 69

The first plenary meeting of the Capital Construction Committee was held at 2 p.m. on the 15th in the auditorium of the Lishi Society. The attending guests and committee members gathered together, making for a grand occasion. The details of the meeting are summarized below:

▲Morning Visit to the Mausoleum

▲Representatives of Committee Members from Beijing and Outside Visit the Mausoleum—At 9 a.m. on the 15th, Committee Member Liu Wendao represented by Dong Xiujia, Committee Member Ge Jingen represented by Yun Weiyou and Wu Bichi, Committee Member He Jian represented by Yuan Hui, and guest Huang Zunzhi and others, went to Zhongshan Mausoleum to pay their respects. They were received by Mr. Zhang and Mr. Huang of the Engineering Department of the Mausoleum Administration Committee. They proceeded to the memorial hall and bowed three times to Premier Sun Yat-sen's portrait, and then retreated in silent reverence. The ceremony concluded and they returned to the meeting; it was already eleven o'clock.

▲Afternoon Opening

▲Venue Arrangement—The venue was the auditorium of the Lishi Society. In the center of the stage hung the party and national flags and the portrait of the late Premier. The words "Capital Construction" were arranged at the front of the stage with pine and cypress. There was a chairman's seat, followed by the committee members' seats, then the seats for those in attendance, and further back, the guests' seats. The orchestra was upstairs, and the recording and press seats were on both sides. Charts and diagrams related to the proposals were posted on the walls on both sides, and potted flowers were arranged all around, making for an orderly and spectacular setup.

▲Committee Members Present—Tan Yankai, Wang Chonghui, Shao Yuanchong, Lin Sen, Wei Daoming, Xu Shiying, Hu Hanmin, Chen Guofu, Chen Shaokuan, Ma Fuxiang, Liu Jiwen, Zhang Nanxian, Kong Xiangxi, Liu Ruiheng, Chiang Kai-shek, Zhu Peide, He Yingqin (represented by Chen Yi), He Jian (represented by Yuan Hui), Lu Diping (represented by Lu Lushan), Liu Wendao (represented by Dong Xiujia), He Chengjun (represented by Tang Zhi), Zhang Qun (represented by Shen Yi), Zhang Zhijiang (represented by Wang Weifan), Wang Boqun (represented by Li Zhonggong), Chen Diaoyuan (represented by Xu Chaotong), Zhang Xueliang (represented by Qin Hua), Chen Mingshu (represented by Yang Zongjiong), Cheng Tianfang (represented by Lai Lian), Sun Ke, Song Ziwen, Yi Peiji (represented by Chen Yu), and expert Mr. McCroskey, among others.

▲Proceedings of the Meeting—The meeting began at 2:10 p.m., chaired by Chiang Kai-shek. After formalities, the chairman gave the opening address. Then, Hu Hanmin, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, and Wang Longhui, representative of the National Government, delivered speeches in succession. After the speeches, Liu Jiwen, Secretary-General of the General Assembly, stood up to report that a total of 25 committee members were present, with three representatives from Beijing and elsewhere, and 15 attendees. To save time, he proposed that the Chairman designate the proposal committee. Thereupon, Chairman Chiang stood up and announced that the meeting had received a large number of proposals, and it was planned to divide them into three groups for review. He then designated the members of the three groups, and the meeting adjourned with music.

▲Chairman's Address—Chairman Chiang Kai-shek stated in his opening address, "The National Government has established its capital in Nanjing for more than three years. Although there are plans for construction matters, the focus has been on making a start. Therefore, the government and the members of this committee hope to build it quickly. In the past two years, the government has opened roads and constructed houses in the capital, which has been criticized by those who do not understand, who believe that the government is too extravagant and disregards the suffering of the people. The government naturally does not pay attention to such baseless arguments. However, the capital is not owned by any one family, nor is it comparable to an ordinary city. It is the center of a country's politics, economy, and culture. If it is not built quickly, it will greatly affect appearances. Currently, matters such as domestic water conservancy and railways have been assigned to responsible parties, but the capital is being neglected. It is not known that if the capital cannot be perfectly constructed, other projects, even if completed, will be in vain. Taking the government's housing needs as an example, matters related to politics and diplomacy are increasing daily. If the old Governor's Office is still used as the residence, it will be impossible. Moreover, ambassadors from various countries are gathering in the capital, which is detrimental to appearances. Therefore, we must strive for construction. Secondly, the problem of tap water has not been realized even after three years of establishing the capital, which is also a major regret. Based on the above situation, I deeply feel that to build the country, we must first build the capital. Nanjing is the place most valued by the late Premier, not only for its beautiful mountains and rivers, but also for its high mountains and plains, making it the most important area in politics, economy, and culture. I hope that this committee will devote its full attention to the construction of the capital, and pay particular attention to its realization."

▲Proposal Review Committee—The first group is responsible for the planning of capital transportation, water conservancy, and ports, as well as the construction of all large-scale engineering projects. The second group is responsible for raising funds for the construction of the capital. The third group is responsible for the consolidation of land and the development of industry, commerce, agriculture, and forestry within the capital area. The members of the first group are Tan Yankai, Hu Hanmin, Wang Chonghui, Sun Ke, Wang Zhengting, Zhang Renjie, Wei Daoming, Chen Shaokuan, Liu Jiwen, Shen Yi, Xu Chaotong, Schubert, Zhuo Yue, Xia Guangyu, Sun Mou, Xu Xinwu, and Liu Baizhou. The members of the second group are Zhu Peide, Yang Shuzhuang, Kong Xiangxi, Liu Luyin, Shao Yuanchong, Wang Boqun, Ma Fuxiang, Dong Xiujia, Tang Yu, Lu Lushan, Yuan Hui, Tao Yougang, Chen Duan, Deng Gang, Jin Guobao, Chen Zhongsheng, and Song Ziwen. The members of the third group are Chen Guofu, Ye Chuqiang, Liu Ruiheng, Yi Peiji, Jiang Menglin, Zhang Nanxian, Xu Shiying, Yang Xiji, Yang Zongjiong, Lai Lian, Zhang Yiou, Gao Bingfang, Liu Youchen, Xu Zhaojun, and Hong Lanyou. The first group is convened by Zhang Renjie, the second group by Kong Xiangxi, and the third group by Chen Guofu.

▲Evening Banquet—Chairman Chiang has scheduled a banquet at the Lishi Society this evening to entertain the attending committee members.

However, because the drugs used have not been scientifically studied, their elements cannot be explored and their effectiveness cannot be expanded. In recent years, foreigners have devoted themselves to this, often taking it as a method to produce new drugs and import them into our country, resulting in a large outflow of profits. It is a pity. The Ministry has now gathered institutions such as the National Central Research Institute to jointly establish the Chinese Drug Research Institute and requested a monthly subsidy of 1,000 yuan to facilitate the process. The resolution was approved. (3) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs reported on the continued allocation of 50,000 yuan in national currency to assist overseas Chinese returning from Russia. The resolution was approved. He Yingqin Arrives in Hankou 71

▲Summoning He Chengjun and Others to Discuss Military Affairs

Hankou Communication: He Yingqin, the director of the Wuhan Branch of the Military Affairs Commission, arrived in Hankou on the 13th at 2 p.m. aboard the China Merchants Bureau's Jiangtian steamboat. Those who welcomed him at the dock included He Chengjun, acting director of the Wuhan Branch; He Guoguang, chief of staff; Wang Lun, deputy chief of staff; Jiang Dingwen, commander of the 2nd Army; Wang Jinyu, commander of the 9th Army; Xu Yuanquan, commander of the 10th Army; Xia Douyin, commander of the 13th Army; Yin Zusheng, fortress commander; Huang Zhenxing, deputy director of the military station; Qian Dajun, education director of the military academy; Wu Xingya, Zhang Guanshi, and Huang Changgui, members of the provincial government; and Liu Wendao, the mayor. After the Jiangtian steamboat docked, He and his wife, Ms. Wang Wenxiang, disembarked and went to the former site of the Foreign Affairs Office to rest. The personnel who came with them included Yu Feipeng, director of the military station; Liu Jianqun, Wang Shi, Yan Kuan, and Leng Xin, counselors; Xie Boyuan, Deng Pingyan, Wu Qi, and Lin Zhiqi, secretaries; Wang Peiren, telegraph operator; Zhou Weigang, Chen Shixu, and Xie Bangqing, staff officers; Wang Wenyan, chief of the management section of the training supervision department; Li Shaoyang, former director of the management office; Xu Xilin, former director of the medical office; Chen Peng and Wan Xiuling, councilors; and thirty-seven adjutants and staff members. A company of military and special affairs transport soldiers also came along. After arriving at the office, He took a short break and then met with various dignitaries. At 4 p.m., he summoned He Chengjun, Wang Jinyu, Xu Yuanquan, Xia Douyin, Jiang Dingwen, Yin Zusheng, Yu Feipeng, Rong Zhenxing, He Guoguang, and others to consult on military affairs and discuss various plans. The meeting lasted for two hours before adjourning. A reporter recently interviewed Mr. He and had the following conversation: (Question) "Director, please tell us the purpose of your visit to Hankou this time." (Answer) "I left Wuhan less than three months ago. I thought that after the Tang rebellion was eliminated, all the elements that had been mobilized and the feudal warlords would be able to turn over a new leaf and no longer dig their own graves. Unexpectedly, Yan and Feng and the reorganized faction, the Western Hills Conference faction, and the Anfu clique have started a rebellion. In order to implement the principles of peaceful reunification, seek the realization of political tutelage and construction, and complete the national revolution as soon as possible, the Central Government has to impose sanctions. My visit to Hankou this time is to take charge of the Wuhan Branch of the Military Affairs Commission under orders and assist Commander-in-Chief He in planning the military campaign." (Question) "What is the strength of Yan and Feng's forces?" (Answer) "The combined forces of Yan and Feng and all kinds of miscellaneous troops are no less than 200,000 men. However, Yan and Feng have deep disagreements and are superficially united and internally divided. Moreover, the replenishment of food, supplies, weapons, and ammunition, as well as spiritual education and training, are far inferior to the Central Army. The Central Army exceeds the rebel army several times, and after years of training and under the command of Commander-in-Chief Chiang, the outcome has already been determined before the battle. At present, our military deployments on the Tianjin-Pukou, Longhai, and Pinghan lines, as well as in western Shandong and northern Hubei, are extremely thorough. Commander-in-Chief Chiang recently personally inspected the front lines, and the morale is even more boosted. The military future is very promising." (April 14)

Reference Materials on the Nepal Incident 73

▲Nepal was founded by a Chinese monk.

▲The first king was Chinese.

▲The people are of mixed Chinese and Indian descent.

▲The Gurkhas cannot represent Nepal.

Translated by the World News Agency from the Indian newspaper "Buddhist India": The origin of Nepal is that those who do not understand its history all say that it became a country after the Gurkhas invaded it in 1786 AD. Therefore, Nepal is the country of the Gurkhas. In fact, this is not the case. All geologists and historians who study Nepal say that during the so-called "Golden Age," Satyaynga, the present-day Nepal Basin, was a lake called Snake Lake. Its first inhabitants came from India. Seven Buddhists visited Si Huayang Pusan and other mountains in Nepal. After these seven Indian monks came, a senior monk named Manjushri Bodhisattva Manjuari came from Mount Wutai in China (translated meaning). After Manjushri came, he drained the water of Snake Lake and opened roads and managed small countries in the valley. Its territory was 14 miles wide, and it was named Manjupattana after Manjushri. This is clearly recorded in the history of Nepal, and the ancient site can still be seen in the modern urban area of ​​Nepal, called McGiput. At that time, a city named Raikabartoni was built in the center of the small country. Its ruins are still in Kashman. According to the famous history of Nepal, Manjushri also introduced fine arts, crafts, agriculture, commerce, and all civilizations from China. Regarding this section, there is the clearest evidence in history that the first king of Nepal was a Chinese prince named Darmakara Dharmasa, who was appointed by Manjushri as king according to public opinion. After the immigrants from China came, they gradually assimilated with the people who moved from India, and their blood mixed, gradually forming a mixed Indian-Chinese nation. Their social religion, customs, and culture are all a mixture of Indian and Chinese, showing distinct characteristics, and creating a new language and a new life situation. To this day, the monosyllabic characteristics of the Nepali language, the white-yellow complexion, as well as art, architecture, social conditions, and intermarriage, are all clear proofs of the integration of Chinese and Indian cultural genes. At that time, a new race, a new culture, a new country, and a new political system were gradually formed in Manjubartoni. The people of China and India were fully unified, and their cultures were fully integrated. So under the leadership of Manjushri, the people publicly elected the Chinese prince Darmakara as the first king, located in the capital Raikabartoni. Because a king ruled two nations and two cultures, in accordance with the meaning of equal rights, the original country name Manjubartoni Nepal Nemapala (or Nebala) Nema means justice, pala or palita means governance or protection, so the name of Nepal is a country governed by equal rights, justice, and fairness.

Important News 2

Qingdao British American Tobacco Company Labor Strike Ends 74

Qingdao Communication: The current labor strike at the British American Tobacco Company in Qingdao was due to the workers' demands for wage increases and job retention, which did not yield satisfactory results. Therefore, they followed the guidance of the company's workers' consolidation committee and continued the strike. The municipal government, however, believed that it had reached an agreement with the British company to resume work on the fourth day, but the workers resisted the order, causing the municipal government to lose credibility with foreigners, which was inappropriate. Therefore, nine representatives were arrested and punished. On the one hand, the municipal party headquarters disbanded the two workers' consolidation committees of the British American Tobacco Company's printing and cigarette making, to prevent them from being used by reactionary elements. On the other hand, it persuaded the workers to resume work as soon as possible. On the 11th, the organizing committees of various political-level trade unions believed that the labor strike at the British American Tobacco Company had been prolonged and was taking extreme directions, which was not a blessing for the local area. Therefore, a joint meeting was held at the municipal party headquarters to jointly guarantee to the municipal government that work could be resumed after the arrested representatives were released, and that there would be no further out-of-bounds actions after the resumption of work. On the 12th, the municipal government and the municipal party headquarters again strictly ordered all workers to resume work as soon as possible. Recognizing the unfavorable environment, more than 1,300 workers had already returned to work on the same day. Those who had not yet returned to work were expected to return to work on the 14th. All conditions would be discussed later. As for the nine arrested representatives, Mayor Ge advocated for strict punishment. Wu Rencang, a member of the municipal party headquarters, is currently mediating the situation and may be released soon. A turbulent labor strike has thus come to an end. (13th)

Taihu Bandits Mostly Dispersed 75

▲Hunan Gang Flees to Zhejiang

▲Linghu Ferry Seized by Bandits

Suzhou Communication: After the bandit Zhang Zhaohua and the Tai Bao A Shu gangs in Taihu Lake were defeated by the bandit suppression army and police forces, it has been learned that the Tai Bao A Shu gang has indeed disbanded and fled in different directions. As for the Zhang Zhaohua gang, after three fierce encirclements and suppressions by the bandit suppression army and police forces, only a hundred or so bandits remain. Yesterday, according to intelligence, twenty or thirty of them fled to Caohe Ganlu Dangkou and other places on the border of Suzhou and Wuxi. Dozens more fled to the Weiting Kunshan area on the 13th. The previous day (the 13th), Xu Boying, captain of the 11th Water Public Security Team, again supervised the patrol boats to Chengcun Lianhua Duo and other places to search for remnants, but found nothing. It was also heard that the county police team stationed in Chengcun went to investigate after the 11th Water Public Security Team exchanged fire with the bandits at Weijing Tang Louzitou, and recovered a machine gun, five or six Mauser pistols, and many rifles abandoned by the bandits on the lake shore, which have been reported to the county government. In addition, after the military and bandits exchanged fire at Chenmu Sanyuan Dam, two rifles and 252 bullets were subsequently recovered and reported to the county for record.

The Zheng Gang, a large gang from Henan, which was staying in Taihu Lake, had a total of fifty or sixty bandit ships. It was heard that the bandits in the Yangcheng Lake area had been dispersed by the military and police, and they were terrified. They have already fled to Zhejiang. At 3 p.m. the day before yesterday (the 13th), the Linghu ferry Dehe of the China Merchants Bureau was sailing through the Shiwai area south of the Sitingzi Port in Zhejiang, when it was seized by the bandits, who took away more than a dozen crew members and passengers, both male and female. Their whereabouts are unknown. The company has reported to Hang Yi, the deputy commander of the Eastern District of the Taihu Bandit Suppression, requesting pursuit and rescue of the hostages.

Li Kunyu, the battalion commander of the 1st Battalion of the 28th Regiment of the Kunshan Bandit Suppression Army, fought fiercely with the bandits at the lotus Duo (i.e., Lianhua Duo) in Yangcheng Lake on the 12th, killing six or seventy bandits (the bandits' bodies have not yet been collected), and captured eight bandits, including Shen Jinshan. The captured bandits were briefly interrogated by Commander-in-Chief Hu in Suzhou on the afternoon of the 14th and then sent to prison for further investigation. The text of the report from the 28th Regiment Commander Yao Chun to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters is transcribed as follows: "Since this regiment was ordered by His Excellency to be incorporated into the Bandit Suppression on the 1st of this month, I immediately ordered the 1st Battalion of this regiment to advance to Bacheng and other places to suppress the bandits as the opportunity arose. According to the report of the battalion commander, this regiment has been ordered to be incorporated into the Bandit Suppression since the 1st of this month, and has been searching the Yangcheng Lake and Dianshan Lake areas. Finally, at 8 a.m. on the 12th, a civilian reported that about a hundred bandits were mooring twelve boats in the Jin-Li Port of Lotus Duo in Xihai Village. After receiving the report, I led the 2nd and 3rd companies and the machine gun platoon to suppress them in three routes. Chen Shiying, the commander of the 2nd Company, led two platoons of soldiers, attached to a machine gun, landed on the north bank of Xiyang Village via Shishi Jing, and used the machine gun to attack the left side of the bandits. Tan Ronglin, the commander of the 3rd Company, led two platoons of soldiers, landed on the south end of Lianhua Duo via Lijia Gu. I led a machine gun and one platoon each from the 2nd and 3rd companies, and attacked the right side of the bandits via Xiba Gate Huangliting. At 11 a.m. on this day (the 12th), we made contact with the bandits at Jin-Li Port. The bandits were defeated and fled to Xiaxiong Tian. I then ordered the 3rd Company to quickly intercept the retreat route of the bandits towards Xiaxiong Tian and implement an encirclement. The street fighting continued until 3 p.m., when the bandits were completely wiped out, and twelve bandit ships, thirty rifles, seven Mauser pistols, two Browning rifles, and a roster were seized. Eight bandits, including Shen Jinshan, Xu Zhenqing, Wang Zhaotai, Qian Wenyuan, Wang Peng, Zhang Xiaoma, Jiang Fangqin, and Xu Zonggui, were captured alive, and thirty-one male and female hostages were rescued. Sixty or seventy bandits were killed, and the remaining bandits drowned in the water. This battle consumed a lot of bullets. I am now sending the bandit prisoners, hostages, and seized items to your headquarters for your inspection."

Local Communication

Jiading 76

The county government held a meeting to stabilize grain prices. On the afternoon of the 12th, the county government convened the district chiefs and the Yicang Bao Ke Committee members, including Jin Boqin, to discuss how to stabilize grain prices. It was resolved that the Yicang Management Committee would purchase 8,000 shi of foreign rice, which would be distributed in six phases starting from June 1st, with each phase lasting ten days. The price was set at 12 yuan per shi, and the distribution of rice to each district would still be handled according to the regulations. The district chiefs were ordered to instruct the township chiefs to compile a list of poor households and report it before May 15th for processing. It was also heard that 3,000 bags of foreign rice had been ordered earlier, and another 5,000 bags of Xiaowen rice had been ordered from Shanghai, to be delivered in April and May, at a price ranging from 6.6 to 6.66 yuan. An application is currently being submitted to the Ministry of Finance for a passport to transport them back.

Fengxian 77

Please Discuss Early Implementation of Grain Sales: People from various districts in this county, due to the recent surge in rice prices and widespread famine, have resorted to using animal feed and grass roots as food. Although announcements about price-controlled grain sales have been repeatedly issued, implementation has been slow, with no commencement date yet. If we follow the precedents of previous years and delay until summer, it is feared that the waters of the West River will not be able to alleviate the plight of the desperate. Therefore, they have jointly requested the county to forward a request to the Righteous Granary Management Committee to expedite the commencement of sales before the registration and investigation are completed, to alleviate hunger. It is reported that the county government instructed the committee yesterday to find a way to implement this urgently.

Levying Sanitation Taxes: The Zhuanghang Business Association has now received approval from the county government to levy a sanitation tax, along with property taxes, within the Zhuanghang district. This tax is specifically for financing sanitation expenses for the entire town and began being collected this month.

Songjiang 78

Minutes of the County Administrative Council Preparatory Meeting: The first County Administrative Council meeting was held last September. Now, half a year has passed. The county government decided to convene the second administrative meeting starting on the 16th of this month. Various bureaus and departments have submitted over fifty proposals. Members include heads of county government departments, bureau directors, and district chiefs as ex officio members. Business, education, and other organizations, as well as local gentry, have been invited by the county government as contractual members. Preparations are complete. A preparatory meeting was held today (the 15th). The opening ceremony will be held tomorrow morning, and discussions will begin in the afternoon. It is reported that among the proposals to be discussed, the more important ones include suppressing rice prices and the construction of a gate on the Yaojing Port, all of which are closely related to the people's livelihood.

Abolition of the District Chiefs' Alumni Association: According to a report from the Jurong County Party Affairs Rectification Committee to the Provincial Party Headquarters, the county's administrative council proposed the establishment of a District Chiefs' Alumni Association. This was considered to be full of feudal ideology and inconsistent with reality, and it was requested that the provincial government be consulted to issue an order to the same administrative offices to abolish it, in accordance with the teachings of Sun Yat-sen. The provincial government approved the consultation and ordered the abolition. This county has also received and is complying with the order.

Training Corps Artillery Regiment Opens in Songjiang: The General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force in Nanjing has dispatched the entire Artillery Regiment No. 2 of the Training Corps of the Central Military Academy to Songjiang to maintain order. The county government recently approved the regiment's official notification and ordered the staff to prepare the headquarters for their arrival. One battalion arrived on the 15th, carrying over thirty steel cannons, dozens of donkeys and horses, and a large amount of baggage. It is reported that two more battalions are expected to arrive in Songjiang tomorrow.

Suzhou 79

Ni Bi and Others Scheduled for Public Trial 80

Ni Bi, Gu Ziyang, Ge Jianshi, former executive members of the Provincial Party Headquarters, and seven others including Chen Boxin, Wang Zhiren, Gu Shuyin, and Ge Shangde, accused of counter-revolutionary activities, were sent by the Provincial Public Security Bureau to the High Court. After two hearings by Presiding Judge Lin Dawen of the First Division, no results were achieved. Judge Lin has now scheduled a public trial for the afternoon of the 25th of this month.

A Member of the Yixing Business Corps Drowns: Near the Dahui Bridge in Xumen, the floating body of a man was found on the (15th) afternoon at approximately 2 PM, coming from the direction of Hengtang Zao Shi Bridge. The District Court sent personnel to investigate and confirmed that the deceased had a symbol and a badge on his chest, identifying him as Zhang Zhenhai, a member of the Yixing Business Corps headquarters. There were no injuries on the body, indicating death by drowning. The corpse was collected by the Tishan Hall.

Water Barriers Installed in Dongshan District: Han Jizhi, the district chief of the seventeenth district of Dongshan, reported to the county government yesterday (the 15th) that he had, together with the police and land security agencies, installed water barriers in the following locations in Taihu Lake: Jiaobai Port, Youche Port, Zhi Port, Tang Port, Yin Jia Port, Qi Xiang Port, Xiao Port, Wu Xiang Port, Xiao Qiang Port, Du Shui Port, and You Shi Jia River Mouth. However, to facilitate the passage of fishing boats, the barriers will not be sealed for the time being, but will be sealed in case of emergency.

Wuxi 81

The Location of the County Court Is Resolved: The county court in this county was previously included in the first phase by President Lin of the Suzhou High Court, and was to be established at the same time as the county courts in Kunshan and Wujin. However, due to funding and location issues, progress was halted. Recently, County Magistrate Sun decided that since the Municipal Preparatory Office has been ordered to be abolished, the original buildings of the Municipal Office are quite spacious. It has now been decided to move the First District Office and the Finance and Construction Bureaus into the former premises, and to move the Public Security Bureau to the original site of the Finance Bureau. The original site of the Public Security Bureau (i.e., the old county government office) will be vacated and allocated as the location of the County Court. This plan has been submitted by County Magistrate Sun to the High Court for approval. President Lin expressed his satisfaction and summoned County Magistrate Sun to Suzhou the day before yesterday to discuss implementation.

Public Security Bureau Resolves Important Cases: Huang Zhenbai, the director of the Public Security Bureau of this county, convened the fifth bureau affairs meeting yesterday, attended by the heads of various branch bureaus. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Preventing counter-revolutionaries from engaging in activities: It was resolved that the heads of each branch bureau would dispatch police to intensify patrols and conduct secret investigations at any time. Special attention would be paid to workshops, river and land terminals, hotels, teahouses, and restaurants within their jurisdictions. (2) Regarding any god-welcoming festivals or similar events within the jurisdiction of each branch bureau, the heads of each branch bureau should dispatch police to dissuade them in advance. If they do not comply, a report should be submitted to the general bureau for investigation. (3) Raising funds to add to the construction of prison facilities: It was resolved that each head of the city district bureau would donate three yuan, each head of the rural district bureau would donate two yuan, and each bureau member and inspector would donate one yuan. These donations will be deducted from their May salaries.

Bandits Rob Two Sailing Vessels in Succession: A sailing vessel from Nanxin Bridge in the northern township set sail towards [the city] from the township at approximately 6 PM the day before yesterday. At 3:30 AM that night, while passing the Kan Zhuang Bridge in Tianxia City, a small rice bun boat suddenly appeared from the opposite direction. Seven bandits jumped out, armed with box cannons, handguns, flashlights, and other weapons. Speaking in the local dialect, they ordered the boat to stop. The owner of the sailing vessel, Cai Rongsheng, realizing the situation was dire, immediately stopped the boat. He was robbed of 18.7 silver dollars, 16,700 copper coins, 15 pieces of white cloth, half of the rice, and clothing and bedding. Passengers on the boat were also searched and robbed. At that time, a Zhutang shuttle boat, sailing from the township to the city, also passed through the area. The bandits boarded the shuttle boat and robbed it in the same manner. After an hour, they carried their loot back to their boat, fired a shot to show their strength, and rowed away. After inspection, it was found that over ten silver dollars, seventy thousand copper coins, a large package of foreign socks, and clothing and food had been robbed. The total loss for both boats was over eight hundred yuan.

Changzhou 82

Transfer of County Court Prosecutor: Xu Heling, the chief prosecutor of the Wuyi County Court and former candidate prosecutor of the Shanghai District Court, was dismissed yesterday by order of the High Court and returned to his original position as a candidate prosecutor of the Shanghai District Court. The vacant position of chief prosecutor of the County Court was filled by Yang Kongyi. Furthermore, Chang Rucheng, a candidate prosecutor of the County Court, was simultaneously ordered to be transferred to the Jiangning District Court as a candidate prosecutor. While Wu Zengshan, the president of the County Court, is on leave, his duties will be temporarily assumed by Judge Tong Jianmo.

Robbery Case Cracked: The Public Security First Division in Wuyi City received a report from Yang Zuo, a resident of No. 6 Dayuan, that his home had been robbed of silver dollars and clothing by a group of bandits. The bureau ordered the police to investigate and successively apprehended the main suspects, Wang Yao, Feng Peide, and the suspected accomplices Chen Hong, Pu Jinsheng, Wang Huaiji, Ma Wenxu, Wang Sheng, and Zhao Yonghe, as well as the stolen silver ornaments, copper coins, and silver dollars. After the victim identified the items as his stolen property, the bureau handed over the suspects and stolen goods to the County Court on the 14th for interrogation. After investigation by the prosecutor, Wang Yao, Feng Peide, Ma Wenxu, Zhao Yonghe, and Wang Huaiji were ordered to be detained, while the others were released.

Danyang 83

Arrest of a Suspected Reactionary: Tang Wencui, a teacher at the County Teachers' Experimental Elementary School, was reported for alleged reactionary activities. County Magistrate Wu dispatched plainclothes judicial police to summon the teacher for interrogation and ordered Fang Weizhou, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, to search his residence for reactionary items as evidence.

Change of Education Bureau Director: Fang Ji-Chen, the director of the Education Bureau of this county, has repeatedly resigned to the Education Department, which has been approved. His position has been temporarily filled by Sun Xinyuan, appointed by County Magistrate Wu.

Commissioned to Collect Silk Products: The National Goods Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has scheduled a National Silk Exhibition in April of this year. With the opening date approaching and this county being a silk-producing area, a special commissioner has been sent to Danyang to collect exhibits.

Zhenjiang 84

Resignation of Water Police District Chief: Deng Zuyu, the district chief of the Fifth District of the Waterborne Provincial Police, who has been in office for over a year, submitted his resignation to the Provincial Government yesterday, the reasons for which are unknown. It is uncertain whether it will be approved.

Zhenjiang Gentry Pleads for Disaster Relief Funds: Local residents Leng Yuqiu, Gan Xiaochuan, Hu Jianchun, Li Songtao, and others, due to continuous drought in the four rural areas of this county in recent years and the locust plague last year, which has worsened the disaster, with people displaced and suffering beyond description, unable to make ends meet, resorting to digging up roots and grass for food, and even selling their children to survive, and also considering that the southwest townships were burned to the ground due to the Big and Small Swords Society incidents, and the Jingxian Mountain area is filled with bandits, making it impossible for travelers to pass, and now facing continuous rain and damaged wheat crops, and the reappearance of famine, with many people starving, petitioned the Jiangsu Provincial Disaster Relief Committee yesterday, requesting that it consider the severity of the disaster and approve the allocation of relief funds to aid the disaster victims.

Yangzhou 85

Merchants Discuss Solutions to Forced Loans: The Yuanmen Bridge and Duozi Street area in this county is a prosperous commercial district. Recently, some former soldiers and disbanded troops, dressed in Western-style clothing, have been forcibly demanding loans from several stores. If they are not granted, they resort to insults and threats, causing widespread panic among the merchants. As a result, the various businesses convened a meeting at the Chamber of Commerce today (the 14th). The unanimous decision was to send a letter to the county government, requesting them to order their subordinates to strictly prevent and protect businesses.

Gaoyou 86

Request to Order the Repair of the Canal Embankment: Dozens of Gaoyou elders, including Wang Zhongjia, are concerned that the Jiangbei Canal Engineering Office is delaying the spring repair of the canal embankment, which affects the lives and property of the lower five counties. Therefore, they jointly petitioned Chairman Ye and Director Sun of the Provincial Government's Construction Department, stating that since the beginning of spring this year, the water level in the canal has been over eight feet, and with the peach blossom flood season approaching and continuous rain expected, the water level is likely to continue to rise. If spring repairs are attempted at that time, it will be impossible to do so. If the canal embankment becomes dangerous, who will be responsible? They earnestly request the Construction Department to review past cases, consider the people's livelihood, and if the funds for this year's spring repairs have been allocated, to send personnel to thoroughly investigate. If the funds have not been allocated, they request that funds be allocated quickly to order the Canal Engineering Office to carry out spring repairs to strengthen the embankment and secure the people's livelihood.

Director Chen Transferred to Yangzhou: Chen Da, the director of the Education Bureau of this county, has been ordered by the Education Department to be transferred to become the director of the Education Bureau of Yangzhou. His position will be filled by Sun Weixian, the director of the Education Expansion Section of the bureau.

Nantong 87

Holding County Political Meeting: Nantong County Magistrate Chen held a county political affairs meeting on the 14th and resolved: (1) Measures to clear up the criminals captured in the Eastern District's bandit suppression, releasing those with minor suspicions and punishing the serious offenders according to the law. (2) The entire county's security force will be trained by coaches sent by the county government. (3) To supplement the strength of the county police force, each police officer will receive an additional yuan in salary.

Provincial Police Force Captures Bandits and Escorts Them to the City: The 13th squadron of the Provincial Police Force suppressed bandits in the second district, killing more than ten bandits and capturing fifteen, including Zhang Xian'en. They were escorted to the city on the 14th and turned over to the Rural Clearing Bureau for interrogation.

Change of Construction Bureau Director: Xiong Yuheng, the director of the Nantong County Construction Bureau, has resigned. The Construction Department has appointed Zhang Ruhong, a technician from the bureau, as the acting director. Yao Pengnian has now been appointed to take over from Zhang Ruhong, who will return to his original position.

Protecting the Outer Sea Fishing Grounds of Tongtai: The nine coastal areas of Hai Tai in Jiangbei are well-known fishing areas in Jiangsu Province. However, due to recent disturbances by sea bandits, fishing boats have been afraid to venture out to sea. The nine fishing associations have joined the Fishery Affairs Bureau to dispatch patrol ships to patrol the sea areas of the two prefectures and protect fishing boats. Starting on the 15th, fishing boats from all ports will be allowed to exit.

Pinghu 88

Executing a Death Sentence After Accepting Bribes to Release Smugglers: He Zan, the former leader of the 3rd squad of the 2nd battalion of the Pinghu Anti-Smuggling Agency, received bribes of 1,820 yuan while in office and released more than 170 smuggling boats into Taihu Lake. Director Jiao Dati discovered this and ordered the police to escort him to Hangzhou for interrogation. Former battalion commander Qiu Qifan and 4th squad leader Gao Qiliang were also implicated, so Qiu and Gao were also escorted to Hangzhou for questioning. The result was that He Zan was indeed the main culprit, and Qiu and Gao were accessories. They were all dismissed from their positions and severely investigated. He Zan, while in prison, instigated a riot among his subordinates, intending to break out of prison. Director Jiao reported this to Commander-in-Chief Chiang, who ordered that he be executed by firing squad outside the Qingbo Gate in Hangzhou on the morning of the 12th.

Pingzha Automobile Road to Begin Construction Soon: The Hangzhou-Pinghu automobile road, from Hangzhou to Zhapu, was completed the day before yesterday and formally opened to traffic. It is calculated that the Zhapu side has already built to Yemao Dun north of Zhapu. From Yemao Dun to the new bridge outside the south gate of Pinghu, the road commissioner and the staff of various neighborhoods are actively carrying out surveying work and investigating the owners of various fields. Construction will begin after the spring harvest. It has been decided to use the east side of the new bridge as the east station.

Hangzhou 89

Announcement of Three Telegraph Bureau Directors: The Zhejiang Telegraph Administration announced yesterday that the Ministry of Communications has appointed Ni Hongtang as the director of the Zhenhai Telegraph Bureau, Huang Binglin as the director of the Haimen Bureau, and Xu Zongtang as the director of the Xiashi Bureau. They were ordered to take office separately and report for record.

Third County Magistrate Examination Held: The Zhejiang Third County Magistrate Examination Committee issued a notice yesterday stating that the examination is scheduled for the 16th. All qualified candidates must report for a physical examination first. However, the application of Hu Hongji was not approved because the certificate he submitted did not have the name of the head of his original agency, making it impossible to verify.

Concrete Measures for Hangzhou Residents' Food Supply: Due to the exhaustion of food supplies in Hangzhou, causing panic, concrete measures have been agreed upon by government, business, and other organizations: (1) The three granaries in the provincial capital will begin selling price-controlled grain no later than May 1st. (2) Representatives of the rice industry will notify rice merchants to go to various places to procure as much as possible to store three months' worth of supplies. (3) The maximum rice price should not exceed seventeen yuan, and rice for the common people will still be sold at thirteen yuan. The rice shops will cover the difference, and sales will be limited to one dou per person. This system will be abolished after the price-controlled grain sales begin.

Xiashi 90

Detailed Report on the Banditry at Tudai Temple: Tudai Town, under the jurisdiction of Tongxiang County, was looted by bandits on the 12th. It is now known that on the morning of that day, more than ten bandits were first sent in disguise to survey the shops and access routes. At about 2 PM in the afternoon, the bandits, wearing red symbols, landed on the east market. First, they cut off the retail telephone line of Zhao Yuanxing's oil mill and deployed sentries. Then, a gunshot was heard, and the bandits attacked, sparing no shops in the Tudai West area. The most significant losses were at the Jin Yuan Chang silver shop, the Lian Lian cloth shop, the Tailong silk shop, the Ni Fuchang rice shop, the Ye Xucheng copper shop, the Xi Yuchang sauce garden, and the Huan Changsheng paper shop, totaling more than thirty stores, with losses of approximately 20,000 yuan. The Gonghe Pawnshop was not robbed because its doors were strong. After obtaining the loot, the bandits set sail. That night, the bandit boat passed through the Beiri Hui Bridge, where it was also heard that they looted again. However, the shops in Tudai that were not looted were still not open for business because they were too frightened. The chief of the local Public Security Bureau was on leave that day, and the patrol leader and others knew that they were outnumbered, so they secretly hid their firearms and the Public Security Bureau's sign, so they were not affected. The water police stationed there, due to their responsibility, resisted the bandits, resulting in a patrol boat being sunk. Afterwards, they went to

pursue them, and sent the 9th company of the 3rd battalion of the 3rd regiment to Zhenjiang to maintain order.

Ningbo 91

Ningbo to Be Assigned to Raise One Million for Construction Bonds: The Finance Department of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, due to insufficient construction funds, issued construction bonds worth ten million yuan, which was approved by the National Government. It is now known that Ningbo City has been assigned one million yuan of these bonds. The Provincial Government has instructed the city government to convene representatives of various industries immediately to engage in fundraising.

New Location for Public Cemetery: Luo, the former mayor of Ningbo, had designated more than 40 mu of farmland originally owned by the Yuyingtang (infant asylum) near the Dahe Bridge in Duantang as the site for the public cemetery. After Yang, the current mayor, visited the site yesterday, he found that the land was low-lying and unsuitable for constructing a public cemetery. After returning to the government office, he instructed the Land Registration Office to find a suitable location.

Yang Shuzhuang Goes to Putuo for Recuperation: Yang Shuzhuang, the chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government and Minister of the Navy, arrived in Ningbo yesterday from Shanghai by transport ship and transferred to Putuo for recuperation. He appeared pessimistic and refused to meet any visitors.

Shaoxing 92

Provincial Order to Reorganize Village Boundary Dispute: The village boundary dispute between Taoxian Village and Nantang Village in Shaoxing has not yet been resolved, which hinders the cause of self-government. County Magistrate Tang has been ordered by the provincial government to instruct Wang Hongze, the self-government instructor of the 9th District, to quickly select an appropriate location and schedule a meeting with the village committees of Taoxian, Nantang, Taoli Six Societies, Ma'an North Village, Ma'an West Village, and Ma'an Mountain Outer Village to discuss reorganization methods.

Request to Implement a Fisheries and Temple Bell Tax: Zhang Daben, a citizen, believes that since the beginning of political tutelage, superstition has not yet been eliminated, which hinders the spirit of self-government. Therefore, he drafted regulations and petitioned the county government to implement a fisheries and temple bell tax, requiring those monasteries and temples with fisheries to pay taxes according to three different rates (five yuan, three yuan, and one yuan), and the people to make donations. It is estimated that the entire Shaoxing area can collect 600 yuan per month. The method is to start with compiling a register and, in addition to paying taxes according to the different rates, each person will be charged a registration fee of one jiao.

First Day of the National Education Conference 93

Opening Ceremony Held... Chairman Chiang Did Not Attend

Welcome Banquet Last Night... General Assembly Opens Today

Chiang Menglin Speaks on the Need for Education to Suit Local Needs

Wu Zhihui Advocates the Promotion of Phonetic Literacy Throughout the Country

Grandeur of the Opening Ceremony 94

In recent days, there has been continuous spring rain in the capital, making the roads muddy and travel extremely inconvenient. On the morning of the 15th, the weather cooperated, the rain stopped, and the sun came out, bringing a sense of invigoration. At noon, the members residing at the Central Hotel were invited to the dining hall for lunch. After the meal, the association prepared cars and sent them to the venue. The members arrived at the venue one after another and went to the rest area in the hall to rest. The opening ceremony began at 2 PM. The various aspects of the ceremony are described below.

A Glimpse of the Venue 95

In the center of the venue was the rostrum, with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen and the national flag of the Kuomintang. The northeast corner of the venue was the music platform, and the southwest and southeast corners were the seats for news reporters and the offices of the affairs and reception departments. The seats were divided into four rows in the center, with the row on the west side reserved for guests and the remaining three rows for members. All the members' tables and chairs were borrowed from National Central University, and covered with white tablecloths, making them quite clean and tidy. A total of 144 seats were set up. In front of the rostrum was the recording seat, equipped with four tables and writing utensils. The entire venue was bright and clean, creating a pleasant atmosphere.

Order of Ceremony 98

At 2:30 PM, the meeting commenced with the ringing of a bell. The Nanjing Special Municipal Government Music Band played music. The master of ceremonies was Rong Weiyang, a staff member. First, everyone stood in solemn silence and sang the Party Song, followed by bowing deeply to the Party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of the late Premier. Then, Chairman Jiang Menglin reverently read the will. The entire venue was silent, and the ceremony was solemn. At 2:45 PM,

▲Jiang Menglin's Opening Address 99

Education Must Emphasize Local Needs

Political Unity Requires Ideological Unity

Esteemed sirs, esteemed representatives, today marks the opening of the Second National Education Conference. We are deeply honored by the presence of representatives from various provinces and expert guests. This conference differs from the first in two key aspects, which I would like to report. (1) Each province has representatives from county and city education bureaus, with the aim of addressing and resolving various local issues. (2) This time, proposals are not submitted by local representatives but are predetermined and assessed by the central government based on current and future needs, and then compiled into a plan. Previous proposals were too broad in scope and difficult to implement, like an encyclopedia of education, leaving one unsure where to begin reading. We hope that this plan can be implemented over the next twenty years. Therefore, what we are presenting this time is of utmost importance, and its success depends on the development of domestic industry and commerce. Once the plan is approved by the central government, we hope that various localities will adapt it to their specific circumstances and strive for progress. Only through the joint efforts of the national education community can we achieve success.

Recently, there has been a great deal of independence within the education sector. (1) There is a tendency towards disorganization, lacking a central pillar of support. In the future, we should adopt a consistent spirit to reform education. (2) Recently, schools and society have failed to communicate, making it difficult for graduates to adapt to the needs of society. This shortcoming is due to education neglecting social conditions. Therefore, despite the expansion of schools, the practical effect is not visible. Recently, some have said that there is no source of economic revenue, and no source of talent. China's education sector seems to be facing this situation. Therefore, we hope that in the future, schools will focus on the needs of the whole society. (3) Lately, those running education have views that are too inconsistent, differing based on the subjects studied or the positions held. As a result, they cannot view national education from a national perspective. In the future, it is imperative that we view national education from a national perspective. (4) Developed countries have comprehensive educational facilities. Rome was not built in a day. Our country should not simply imitate foreign countries step by step. We must determine steps that are suitable for our country to ensure their applicability.

Therefore, this plan aims to remedy these shortcomings, establish a common standard and proceed in an orderly manner. However, education relies on political stability. Therefore, on the one hand, we should create a center of governance so that the people of the whole country can focus their will and unify their spirit. On the other hand, we should create an academic center so that the thoughts of young people are unified, preventing them from being led astray. From this perspective, we should have a unified governance and a unified ideology, so that we can be like the North Star, around which all the stars revolve, as the ancient saying goes. Finally, we must remember Premier Sun Yat-Sen's last instruction: "Peace, struggle, save China."

▲Tan Yankai's Admonition 100

Hope for Systematic Methods

May All Localities Comply and Implement

Today marks the beginning of the Second National Education Conference. Although the resolutions of the First National Education Conference were numerous and detailed, they were difficult to implement. Therefore, this Second National Education Conference will begin with a plan predetermined by the central government, which will be more systematic, so that everyone can come here and discuss it in detail. Currently, all parties hope to produce systematic methods so that all localities can comply and implement them. If we can do this effectively, there is hope for the future.

Wu Zhihui's Speech 101

Advocate Paying Attention to Literacy

The inadequacy of Chinese education is due to the failure of the older generation to implement proper measures. As one of the old guard, and about to become a historical figure, I dare to make a humble request to scholars across the nation. The request is a small matter. Let me briefly explain it to you all. China cannot compete with other countries because of insufficient knowledge. However, I believe it is due to a lack of method. With a method, one can seek knowledge. For example, the theory of relativity, as long as there is a method to understand it, then even the theory of relativity can be understood. In the current discussion, (at this time, Mr. Wu took out a distribution chart indicating the proportion of literate and illiterate people) there is a question about adult literacy education. Recalling one day, a Japanese person said to me, "Recently, the number of literate people in China is only 35 percent. The number of literate people in Japan is 95 percent." A few days ago, Mr. Liu Zhan'en attended the World Education Conference, and foreigners asked him about the number of literate people in China. Mr. Liu replied that it was 20 percent. I believe that these illiterate people can also live in society, but ultimately they cannot control their environment as well as literate people. If we want to promote things, teaching people to read can start with phonetic symbols. Phonetic symbols had two major shortcomings in the past: (1) From the time of their promotion, the government did not first understand phonetic symbols themselves, so promoting them among the people was not very effective. (2) Everyone regarded phonetic symbols as characters. Today, when we promote phonetic symbols, they are only annotations beside Chinese characters so that illiterate people can recognize Chinese characters after learning phonetic symbols. For example, the phrase "not recognizing characters is very difficult." Everyone should quickly think of a method to recognize characters. Annotate words like this with phonetic symbols, and post them near train stations as a substitute for slogans. This will allow those who already know phonetic symbols to recognize the characters. Recently, many people feel a headache when they see phonetic symbols, or they may think so in their hearts even if they do not say it out loud. In fact, alphabets were invented before the Zhou Dynasty. The Phoenicians had alphabetic characters. For example, (1) the character for "one" evolved from the shape of an owl and became pronounced as "aleph". (2) The character for "two" evolved from the shape of a heron and became pronounced as "beth". After Phoenician characters entered Greece, they became today's English letters. After entering Hebrew, they became today's Hebrew alphabet. Today, Turkey is reforming its writing system and is changing the letters of the Hebrew alphabet. Phonetic symbols are not characters themselves but are used for phonetic transcription. If phonetic symbols were characters, then Russia also has an alphabet, so why are 75 percent of the people still illiterate? This shows that characters are a tool for seeking knowledge, not that phonetic symbols can have their effect. Phonetic symbols only help with literacy. Characters and phonetic transcription are two different things. Our country already has characters today, but it lacks a phonetic transcription system. Today, when we teach illiterate people characters, if we teach them 2,000 characters, 1,000 characters, or 600 characters, they will ultimately not be able to apply them. If we teach them phonetic transcription, then they can pronounce and recognize any character they see in the future. Japan has a literacy rate of 95 percent. I think this is the number of people who know the alphabet. If it is the number of people who know Chinese characters, then I dare say it is only 35 percent. When we compare ourselves to them, we find that the number of people who know the alphabet is not as high as in their country. When Japan interacted with our country, they would often write things like "The emperor of the land where the sun rises" changed to "The emperor of the land where the sun sets." This shows that they had learned our writing. Japan used Chinese characters to create katakana and hiragana, adopting our country's methods of "pronounced like 'a'" and "pronounced like 'pei'" for pronunciation. Japan does not value our country, but it does not abandon Chinese characters. This shows that characters cannot be hastily abandoned. In the future, when we promote phonetic symbols, we should also annotate Chinese characters with letters so that those who do not know Chinese characters can also read. However, when promoting it, it must start with you all, gentlemen. It only takes a little time to recognize. The function of phonetic symbols has two purposes: first, to unify language. The four characters "Da Xue Zhi Dao" (The Great Learning) can be read in the same way by people from Guangdong, Sichuan, Shanghai, and Beiping. Second, it is convenient for women. These phonetic symbols are nothing short of teachers for all classes of society, and they can provide the tool of literacy to the illiterate throughout the country.

▲Minister Kong's Speech 102

▲Hope School Education Can Be Practical 103

Kong Yongzhi gave a speech, "I participated in the Capital Construction Committee meeting, so after that meeting, I came here to attend. Minister Jiang firmly urged me to speak. Since this opportunity is rare and talents are gathered, I would like to share my views with you all. Universal education is an important goal today. I believe that education must be practical. In recent years, Chinese education has been full of empty talk and lacks practicality. China's industry is lagging behind others. Looking at imported goods, regardless of cars, trains, foreign cloth, or foreign paper, they all come from foreign countries. Other things like Sunkist oranges and Washington apples also flood the markets. Looking at exported goods, China only accounts for 14 percent of the silk exported to the United States, while Japan accounts for 85 percent. This situation is very dangerous. The way to change this is to make school education practical. Therefore, one way to save the country today is to seek the universality of education, and especially to seek the applicability of education. American school education has a method of reading for two weeks and experimenting for two weeks. I hope that China can also emulate it today. In the future, China's implementation of education must focus on increasing production. The colleagues of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce are very willing to accept your valuable opinions."

▲Anhui Education Bureau Compiles and Prints Reports to Give to Members 118

Cheng Tianfang, the director of the Anhui Education Bureau, has been in charge of education in Anhui for more than a year. During this year, he has actively and tirelessly carried out the rectification and expansion of education in the province, such as increasing education funding, implementing inspections and guidance, reforming editing and publishing, expanding the number of schools and organizing their content, holding various meetings and various examinations, promoting physical education and the Boy Scouts, and promoting social education and county compulsory education. During the past year, there have been considerable achievements in all of these areas. Now, Mr. Cheng wants to publish the progress of Anhui education over the past year openly to society, so that those in the country who care about education can understand the situation of Anhui education and offer criticism. He ordered the various departments and sections under his jurisdiction to collect materials in February of this year, and the translation and compilation office compiled them into a volume entitled "Anhui Education in the Past Year". The entire book is divided into two parts: Part A is the department's work section, describing the department's work progress in the past year, the revision of laws and regulations, the planning of education funding, the liquidation of school property, personnel appointments and removals, inspection and guidance, the rectification of academic style, the expansion of provincial education, academic culture, physical education, various meetings, and various examinations. Part B is the section on the general situation of education, describing the general situation of education in the province in the past year and the general situation of local education. The general situation of education in the province is further divided into higher education, secondary education, primary education, and social education. The book has now been published and is approximately one thousand several hundred pages long, a thick volume bound in hardcover. It can be called a monumental work among the publications of domestic education administrative agencies. With the opening of the National Education Conference approaching, it is heard that the department has specially prepared one hundred copies for distribution to the members attending the meeting.
