Laughing It Off 211

— Sea Traveler

▲ Teacher (Preparing to explain the meaning of "brother-in-law" to the students): Children, do you have an older sister?

A student: Sir, she already has three lovers. There's nothing you can do about it.

▲ Woman A: His marriage to her is not a good match because he's too short, and she's too tall.

Woman B: It doesn't matter. They're very loving. Haven't you noticed that she never wears high heels anymore?

▲ A: Who was that person you were just talking to? What's your relationship with him?

B: He's a distant relative.

A: A very distant relative?

B: You could say very distant. We have fourteen siblings. He's the oldest brother, and I'm the fourteenth and youngest. Isn't that very distant?

▲ A: I'm so sorry. I really didn't know you were coming to my humble abode today. Otherwise, I would have prepared some better food and wine.

B: Don't worry about it. Next time I come, I'll give you a telegram in advance.

▲ A: I've married your younger sister this time. Your family must be very lonely. Do you hate me?

B: What are you talking about? The moment she married, I felt like a huge weight had been lifted off my shoulders. I'm more grateful than anything. How could I hate you?

Random Notes After Liang Zhongjia's Death 212

— Fan Xiang

Russia insulted us, humiliated our national sovereignty, and invaded our territory. I sent Liang Zhongjia to lead troops to defend against them. Unfortunately, he returned and suddenly died. The whole country mourned together, sighing and lamenting. Yesterday, my old friend Mr. Huang told me some random notes after Mr. Liang's death. I'm writing them down immediately.

Mr. Liang's death was due to cardiac paralysis. When he was dying, he had already lost consciousness. His breathing was erratic, and he suddenly died at 7:40 AM on the 8th inside the Manhai Garrison Headquarters. His groom, Lin, was attending to him and was the first to discover it. By nearly ten o'clock, the news spread throughout the city. The citizens cried out, "General Liang is dead!" They wept loudly, as if they had lost their parents. At that time, the sky was overcast, with a cold wind blowing. The coolness was piercing. Around 1 PM, there was a torrential downpour, as if the heavens were also shedding tears of sorrow. Alas.

Mr. Liang had a famous horse that he always rode. Since his death, the horse has been neighing sadly all day long, neither drinking nor eating. The horse seems to know and grieves for the loss of its master.

Mr. Liang was generous and righteous, always helping the poor and rescuing the distressed. Therefore, his subordinates wept and lamented upon hearing this tragic news. His groom, Lin, cried especially grievously and fainted three times. Mr. Liang's posthumous love was so touching. Alas.

When Mr. Liang was dying, he was wearing a woolen shirt, an undershirt, and a felt blanket. The quilt he was covered with was also only made of cotton. After his death, some people were sorting out his belongings and found a package on the side of the bed. It was wrapped in white paper, with the words "Souvenir" written in blood on it. Upon inspection, it was an eight-inch-long sharp blade. The discovery of this blade suggests that Mr. Liang used to appear on the battlefield, advancing and retreating in a hail of bullets. His bravery in annihilating the enemy cannot help but command our respect.

A Record of a Guest's Excursion to Scenic Spots (Part 2) 213

— Bai Xi

The evening was approaching. Mr. Rong Desheng, the garden's owner, along with Jinshi Qian Mingshan from Wujin, and the couple Gu Qiaoruo and Zhang Jinyun, all happened to be in the garden. They entered the banquet together, and during the banquet, they spoke at length about the suffering that the press and the industry have endured in recent years. Everyone sighed in unison. As the banquet came to an end, it was almost the first drumbeat of the night. The guests all stayed in the garden, while the rest of us returned to the city. The next day, the garden's owner hired the Yang's painting boat to take the guests to tour the lake quickly. He pre-arranged for me and Tiao Fu to wait in the city. After the Tang and Yu couple and Qiaoruo and others boarded the boat, they would sail to the Yuanzhu to wait. Jiezi and the guests went directly to the Meiyuan because Meiyuan is only separated from Yuanzhu by a body of water, so the guests could wander around early. As soon as the boat arrived, they would have a meal. Then they drove to the newly developed Liyuan by Mr. Wang. The time was not wasted, and the tour was leisurely. Unexpectedly, when we arrived at Yuanzhu, it was almost noon. We searched all over the Flying Cloud Pavilion, Guangfu Temple, and Xiaohangu, but there was no trace of the guests. We met Mr. Chen Siming and Mr. Yang Rongchun at Hengyun Villa. They inquired that the guests had not arrived. So they decided to wait on the boat. Mengdie showed Qiaoruo the Acacia Bean Poem of He Jiezi. I also corrected the Sea Tang Poem Under the Moon with the same seat. I learned that Mr. Tang Moubo was also good at chanting. I asked for a five-character poem about his trip to Ganlu Temple. I was surprised to see that it was well received. Ms. Qingtang even asked her two young sons to recite Tang poetry and sing for fun. Their voices were loud and clear, skilled and rhythmic, which shows that the Tang family has a deep foundation in learning. (Moubo is the eldest son of Mr. Weizhi) It is appropriate to have such a Ningxin. Yu Jun is a great educator. His usual training is very effective. Soon a phone call came saying that the guests were all waiting for the ferry at Wanqingtang. Tiao Fu drove a steamship to greet them. After a while, a leaf-like boat came flying through the waves. They were all happy to have waited for a long time. They discussed entering the table first. Half drunk, Ms. Huanfen led the tour of Yuanzhu. Back on the boat, they enjoyed the rest of their feast. The boat went straight to Liyuan. Liyuan is located in the shade of Wuhu, facing the water and facing the mountains. The scenery is secluded and beautiful. Mengdie and I described its twists and turns as elegant, like the writing of Zhenchuan. The momentum of Yuanzhu is relatively strong, which can be compared to Yuju. Meiyuan is beautiful and complete, which is the poem of Yuxisheng. After the tour, they returned to Meiyuan for a short rest. Jiezi set up a banquet at Taihu Hotel to continue the unfinished joy. We returned to the city. It was late at night. The next morning, Tang and Yu invited them to lunch, and they also arranged to visit the People's College and Wangxiang Experimental Area run by Yu Jun. I was mistaken by the messenger and did not participate in the visit. It is a pity. However, according to the oral description of Mr. Zhuping, the old women in Wangxiang can read. Even the poorest families can pay attention to cleanliness. The merit of Yu's education can be verified by these two points. Zhang returned to Shanghai that afternoon. Before leaving, he earnestly talked about the relationship between the industry and the press. He had especially great insights into the plan to develop the scenic spots of Wuxi. This trip of Zhang will be a benefit to Xiyi, not just sightseeing. This is the record.

A Record of the Noise in New York 214

— Ji Jin

A guest returned from the New World, saying that the streets around Broadway in New York were bustling and bustling, especially in the commercial and industrial areas. The whirring of cars and the rattling of factories were earth-shattering and incessant day and night. Those who enter it are invariably affected by this major sound wave and gradually become deaf. Moreover, the majority of these were laborers. According to a report this spring by Mr. Gan Erte, chairman of the New York Noise Prevention Committee, noise has a significant impact on the human body's blood circulation, heart beating, and brain movement. According to a recent survey of laborers, car drivers, boilermakers, and machinists in the city who suffer from noise-induced hearing loss, there are 83,000 people, accounting for about 73 percent. Among them, the number of people suffering from noise-induced hearing loss in the four years from 1925 to 1929 was more than half as many. If this continues, not only will these people's ears be completely deaf, but, as mentioned above, it will also greatly hinder their physical and mental development.

It is impossible to make machinery silent because of deafness. As for cars, the timing of their sounds may be slightly restricted, but it is ultimately dangerous and inconvenient for pedestrians. According to people in the meeting, there are no less than a thousand factories in New York City. The smoke is heavy, and there are often flying debris that penetrate the eardrum and accumulate and block it for a long time, which is enough to form deafness. This is especially obvious. The council is now paying very close attention to various factories for the sake of preventing noise. It is expected that there will be major changes in special characteristics in ten years. Otherwise, New York will become a deaf city in the world.

▲ Short Message: Since Bai Longshan Ren assumed the position of principal of Changming Art School, he has been going to the school every Wednesday to explain painting techniques and revise students' homework. This week, he went to Ning because of something, so he went to make up the class on Friday. After the class, he passed by the Western painting classroom and saw that there were various facilities for displaying still life and animal life writing. He took a Western painting pen and Western painting paint and did still life painting on the Western painting cardboard on the easel. It was his first time trying the pen, although he was not proficient, the color and brushwork were still very flavorful. The students of the whole school craned their necks and watched from afar, all of them dancing with joy. This is truly an unprecedented fun writing for the old man's life and a grand event in the Shanghai art world.

Random Notes from Shenyang 215

— Shen Tingkai

I went to Dalian in early spring. I admired the name of Shenyang and made a small trip there. I have a few trivial things to write down.

There are many sugar fruit and tea food shops in the provincial capital. As far as the eye can see, there are a total of thirty-one Daoxiangcun stores. I remember that the Daoxiangcun stores in Shanghai and Jiangzhe inland are also not insignificant. Most of them are operated by Suzhou merchants, and they are crowned with the words "Gusu Daoxiangcun". However, Shenyang is just the opposite. Only two or three stores are crowned with the word "Gusu". Although they are also operated by people from the south, most of them are from Shaoxing instead of Suzhou. Therefore, in the future, people with good taste outside the customs will gradually know the ancient Yue but not Jin Chan. And the words "Gusu Daoxiangcun" that we often see in our eyes, will they gradually be changed to "Ancient Yue Daoxiangcun"?

Southern Seas Travelogue (14) 216

— Linghua

Miss Li Cibei, who traveled with us, suffered from seasickness and vomiting. Besides Mr. Chen, she had no other Chinese to look after her. Mr. Chen was very worried because as the boat sailed west of Singapore, there were fewer and fewer Chinese on board, and it would still take twenty-eight days to reach Marseille, France. Mr. Chen and I both disembarked in Singapore. We felt a bit like leaving Yangguan Pass without a single friend. Mr. Chen is a Christian and is enthusiastic about everything. He gives money and effort in every way possible. Everyone who travels with him benefits from his help, and he is especially considerate in looking after Miss Li, which is very rare. Li is also a Christian. The two often teased me about Buddhism. I acknowledged it and argued with them, saying, "Today's Buddhists are mostly lazy, Indianized types. Compared to the clean, diligent, and courageous Christians, they have benefited much more from Jesus's sacrifice. However, Buddhism should evolve and work with the common people. Getting rid of its corruption and laziness would be beneficial, as its strengths are still significant. Who can say that Buddhists will ultimately be useless? Only those who sit around eating and claiming to be teachers of gods and men are burdens on society." Thus, the fate of idols and monks representing Buddhism is coming to an end, and a scientific, popularized Buddhism will rise in its place.

During our conversation, Mr. Chen suddenly said, "What you say is true. I have been in Burma for a long time and know that the trend of Buddhism in Burma has also changed greatly in recent years." I asked, "How so?" He said, "There are two Burmese monks named Uya. One of them is fluent in English and French and has repeatedly campaigned for independence, resulting in several imprisonments. I heard he has now fled to China and will go to Russia. Another monk, also named Uya, is currently resisting the British government. He went on a hunger strike in prison for sixty-seven days to arouse the sympathy of the Burmese people and died in prison. Hundreds of thousands of Burmese people held a large memorial march. Even Gandhi from India sent people to participate in the meeting and jointly resist," he said. I replied, "You see, Buddhists are not entirely passive, and Indianization is not entirely passive. Looking at the one death and one escape of these two monks, it seems there is still something that can be done."

In the afternoon, the ship issued an order for everyone to practice with lifebuoys. This involved hanging four pieces of light wood in a hemp bag around the neck, roughly like the ammunition pouches carried by soldiers. All passengers of third class and above had to practice, men, women, old, and young, lining up for roll call. Instructors provided training. Smaller ones were used for children, and women with babies hung them around the babies' necks. However, there is an important maritime rule that must be followed. In an emergency, men are not allowed to rush to disembark first. The captain has the authority to use a handgun to direct women to disembark first to escape. If a man mistakenly tries to go first, he will be shot with a handgun. This is the maritime rule. This point also reflects Kunhua's doctrine, valuing gentleness over strength, preferring to sacrifice the strong to protect the gentle, embodying humanitarianism. I have two feelings about this. The Sixth Patriarch said to the Fifth Patriarch, "Get on the boat, and I will ferry you across." The Sixth Patriarch took the oar and said, "When confused, the teacher ferries us across. When enlightened, we ferry ourselves across." Now, in the lifebuoy, only self-ferrying is possible. Only those who can ferry themselves can ferry others. If you don't have the strength to support yourself, you can't rely on other forces at this time. Another feeling is that passengers of third class and above have lifebuoys, while passengers in steerage below have no lifebuoys. The value of life is truly determined by money. Isn't that a great injustice?

European Travel News (50) 217

— Liu Haisu

▲Modern Theater Decoration (Middle)

The decoration of twentieth-century theaters has reached a point where it must change direction. The main reason for this change is that the theater has gradually lost its non-personalized stage setting nature and become a collective character, incorporating the writer, the actors, and the audience.

This is to create an environment, an atmosphere. Without this, the drama cannot leave a lasting impression. On stage, as on the screen, action and rhythm should find a precise and structured position in this atmosphere.

Therefore, the decorator's job is to constantly make the decoration a consistent harmony, avoiding poverty and dryness, to eliminate the audience's antipathy.

When listening to a classical drama, such as Esther, decoration is of little concern and can almost be ignored. This is because, according to the conventions of classical drama, the audience stands outside the performing events. He listens, watches, and comments, without any action. This is written dialogue literature, which is expressed more clearly by the stage scenery, plus a little decoration and costume "explanation."

Modern drama is no longer like this. The script, actors, and director should be integrated and completely closely matched to create a strong atmosphere and focus the audience's attention, and to make the audience forget themselves and be in the situation of the characters in the play, especially to create a collective movement, so that the audience cannot but be one of them. To achieve this goal, the script and actors are important, but the decoration must be one step further. In other words, decoration is especially important.

This tendency is not only true in drama. The same movement occurs in all arts. The author of a novel does not tell a story to the reader, but makes the reader feel that he is the protagonist. The painter unfolds his picture in front of the audience, not saying, "This is nature. I copied it down for you," but saying, "Look how strange and beautiful this nature is..."

Therefore, today's drama no longer just mixes "action," "words," "scenery," and "decoration" equally, but tends to unity so that people are no longer satisfied with reading a script, but must listen, see, and confirm, that is, to make the audience also live in it. These elements were previously hostile, and few people ever intended to unify them. The power of these elements is born with other forces. This so-called "other force" is not easy to determine, but it plays a huge role in your unconsciousness. Then what is this "other force" and where does it come from?

Is it from the actors? That's rare. Today we have few people like Sarah Bernhardt, Duse, or Mounet-Sully.

Is it from the author? No, it's the decorator. If it is the work of O'Neill, Toller, or Lenormand, then the decoration is only a by-product of the work. The decorator can only follow step by step. There are also Shakespeare and Molière's plays, which can be performed in front of dark walls without feeling the need for decoration. But if the script is not obvious, then it completely depends on the decoration. It can be said that nine-tenths of it is the decorator's business. He can make the abilities of the author and actors more prominent.

Ford Motor's Style Change · Ding · Zu · Ze 236

▲ Stainless Steel Replaces Nickel Plating

▲ Radiator Changed to a Narrow and Long Style

▲ Adoption of Small Wheels and Large Tires

▲ Body Style Made More Beautiful

Ford Motor, in order to maintain its position of low prices and massive production, does not change its style as frequently as other cars. For example, the Model T Ford continued its style for more than ten years until it was changed to the Model A in 1928. The Model A has been in production for two years now, and there are now plans for another change, which have already been implemented and are already on sale in the United States. However, there is still no news of this new car being shipped to China.

This time, the change in Ford's car is not in the actual mechanical parts. Only slight improvements have been made to the appearance of the body. Therefore, companies that manage Ford Motor in various regions will not be affected by unsold vehicles, except for customers who tend to be trendy.

The most notable feature of the 1930 new Ford Motor is the use of stainless steel to replace the nickel-plated parts. According to the decorative beauty of the car body, the first requirement is a refined style, and the second requirement is brilliant color. The paint used by each car is now Duco paint. There is no special new paint. The metal parts on the other car bodies have always used nickel plating. By 1928, many cars had changed to nickel plating. The color of cadmium is cyan-white, which is more radiant than nickel. However, the Model A Ford did not follow other cars and imitate it, but still used the old nickel plating. The public thought that Ford was too old-fashioned. In fact, with Ford's financial resources and manufacturing capabilities, although the value of cadmium is slightly more expensive than nickel, it is not impossible to use cadmium plating. Ford is quite revolutionary in manufacturing and does not want to follow in the footsteps of others. This time, it resolutely used stainless steel and abandoned nickel and cadmium plating, which is the first in the automotive manufacturing industry. In the future, other cars will definitely imitate Ford Motor's use of stainless steel.

New Ford Motor Six-Window Four-Door Sedan

Stainless steel is a kind of alloy, and its color is like white tin. Neither humidity nor acidity can make it rust. Its quality is firm but not brittle, and it is ductile. It can be hammered into various styles. Its radiance is soft, not as irritating as chromium. Moreover, nickel plating and chromium plating only apply a thin layer of nickel or chromium to the metal. After many frictions, the applied nickel or chromium will disappear one day. Stainless steel does not have this drawback. According to the modern metallurgical industry, there is an alloy called stainless steel. Its properties are similar to stainless iron, but due to the difficulty of manufacturing and the high value, it is not noticed by the automotive manufacturing industry except for the manufacture of high-quality knives and forks. Ford Motor's use of stainless steel this time is said to be a new discovery of the factory. The manufacturing cost is not expensive, but the manufacturing method is extremely secret, so the outside world does not know its composition. Even in Dearborn, where the Ford factory is located, it is only known that the new term for this stainless steel is Allegheny Metal.

New Ford Motor's shiny parts of the car body, such as the radiator shell, the lampshade, and the wheel hub, are all made of stainless steel. The novelty of its color is a prominent feature in today's car team.

Secondly, the changed part of the Ford Motor is the radiator. Its style is narrower and longer than the old one, which adds a lot of beauty. The other is the use of small wheels and large tires. The current tire size is 29X4.75 inches. The style of the car body is that after the radiator is raised, the waistlines on both sides can be drawn into a straight line from the front of the car to the rear of the car. The length of the car body has not increased, but after the short line of the car neck, the inside of the car body is slightly wider than before.

In addition to the usual six styles of the new Ford Motor, namely two convertibles and four sedans, a new six-window sedan has been added.

A Record of the Merger of the Two Major Gasoline Companies in the United States · Cheng · Zhi · Zheng 237

▲ Mobil and Vacuum Companies Merge

▲ The Gasoline Market Feels a Major Threat

We may all know that there are two great kerosene companies in the United States. One is Mobil and the other is Vacuum. The capital of both companies is exceptionally strong, and almost all have branches everywhere. Now, a piece of good news tells us that these two major companies have actually merged. After this incident was spread, the gasoline market suddenly changed dramatically. The impact of the waves is bound to have a major impact. Therefore, without hesitating to use words, I will record the details of this merger and tell you, the readers.

Originally, the merger of Mobil and Vacuum had been brewing for a long time. After several months of negotiation, the board of directors of both parties decided on this issue. Speaking of the nature of these two companies, there is indeed a possibility of cooperation, because the products of the New York Mobil Line are mostly made of crude oil and refined into motor oil and kerosene. The Vacuum Company is a well-known producer of machine oil. Most of the lubricating oil used on machines everywhere is supplied by it. Mobil's business is mainly in the United States, while Vacuum's business is mainly overseas customers. These two differences further highlight the need for mutual support. These two major companies have a very long history and have established a very solid foundation overseas. Vacuum's branches are in Australia, Egypt, South, East and West Africa, and Europe. Mobil's power has not reached these places, but it has extremely large oil storage pools in the Far East, Near East, and India. In this way, once the two parties merge, their power can reach the entire globe.

Page 20

In the United States gasoline market, the merger of the two companies is especially meaningful, because the modern business trend is to focus on one company while supplying various products at the same time. In other words, everything from crude to fine and other products should be managed by one company. In this way, the products can obtain considerable economies and compete with the same industry. Originally, Mobil and Vacuum each had its own strengths and weaknesses. The short-sightedness is that Mobil is not good at engine oil and Vacuum lacks fine products. Now that the two companies are merged into one, these difficulties will naturally be solved. Mobil has a recent plan to use all its strength to develop motor oil, because its importance today is indisputable. Because of the development of automobiles, gasoline has also become an indispensable fuel. In the past, because it was restricted by other products, it was not able to concentrate its energy on seeking the great development of gasoline. Now, Vacuum is in charge of other products, and Mobil can naturally have no worries. At this moment, it is planning an internal reorganization and paying attention to the national advertising plan.

What will be the situation after the merger? First, the new company's power will reach 9% of the national oil consumption, and it can be equal in strength to the rest of its major competitors. The situation abroad is similar. After the merger agreement was concluded, the government was also requested to file a record. The government sent it to the court for review. After the two companies were allowed to merge, they were renamed General Petroleum Corp. General Petroleum can have all the assets of the two companies. The company will issue new shares separately. All old shares of Vacuum can be exchanged for three new shares. Mobil shares will be exchanged for new shares at the same price. The board of directors will be re-elected, but the number of people from both companies must be equal. Among the assets, goodwill is the most valuable item. Other trademarks are also very impressive. The so-called goodwill is the company's reputation, which can also be said to be the brand. This kind of thing is empty and nothing, but it happens to be the most valuable. This is common in the United States.

From the above, it can be seen that the merger of the two major companies in the United States can have a lot of influence. As far as the company itself is concerned, the two sides support each other and adjust each other. It is extremely powerful to resist external competition. In the gasoline market, all colleagues naturally feel a great threat after hearing the news of the merger, because they can clearly see that a strong enemy has come again. As for users, they may be able to obtain many conveniences as a result. The more intense the competition in the same industry, the better the prices will be. Even if the price is not cheap, at least the service must be satisfactory. Therefore, from the standpoint of our users, we absolutely express our 12-minute approval of the merger of the two companies.

Ford Motor Creates New Record 238

▲ Driving Non-Stop for 500 Hours

▲ Traveled a Total of 14,540 Miles

Ralph Ansby and Henry Slisha of Cincinnati held a non-stop driving event for 500 hours on a half-mile mud track, setting a new world record for automobiles.

The drivers traveled a total of 14,540 miles in 500 hours, without even leaving the Model A Ford roadster they were driving. The previous automobile record on a half-mile mud track was 440 hours. Ansby and Slisha even surpassed the 490-hour record of motorcycles. The driving started at 8:25 pm on November 12 and stopped at 4:25 pm on December 3. The average speed was 35 miles per hour.

Ansby and others telegraphed the Detroit Ford Motor Company, saying that this time driving the Ford Motor was to conduct various tests of strength and to experience various weather conditions, mostly rain, cold, and snow. The Ford Motor always showed its perfect operation. We firmly believe that this car can withstand another 500 hours of punishment. We are very honored to create this new record with the Ford Model A car. It also said that the drivers were also subjected to tests of endurance. We all feel very good, but sitting in the car for 500 hours is not without fatigue and numbness.

Miscellaneous Records

Scenic Spots Along the Xiutun Road · Zhuo 242

The Wutun Motor Road is under construction. It began in the spring of last year. Jixi, Shexian, and Xiuning are carrying out construction in separate sections. From Jixi to Shexian, there are over a hundred li. The roadbed has been completed. From Shexian to Tunxi, there are fifty li, and the roadbed has also been completed. Later, due to the disturbances caused by Bao Gang's defeated soldiers in southern Anhui and the lack of funds, it was not possible to open the road to traffic. However, the section from Tunxi eastward to Xiuning City, which is thirty li, was opened to traffic last month. Business is very prosperous, with four round trips each day, which is quite convenient. It is recently heard that the section from Tunxi eastward to Caoshi, which is fifteen Chinese li, will also be opened to traffic soon. It is expected to become even more convenient. It is said that Tunxi is an important town in southern Anhui and the center of the old six counties. Its commercial prosperity is no less than that of Wuhu. Last year, it was ravaged by the bandit Zhu Laowu, and the entire town was reduced to ashes. According to the investigation by the Tunxi Post-Disaster Relief Committee, the losses were estimated at no less than twenty or thirty million yuan. However, since the disaster, reconstruction has been underway in an orderly manner. It was not expected that it would take a hundred years to recover. In the recent period, it has already become quite impressive. Therefore, the ancient sites and scenic spots along the Tunxi-Xiuning Motor Road are briefly recorded as follows: (1) About five li from Tunxi, it is the first station from Xiu to Tun. The place is called Longfu, which is the hometown of Dai Dongyuan, who assisted in compiling the Siku Quanshu during the Qianlong era of the Qing Dynasty. The site where Dai Dongyuan studied still exists. Some time ago, Huang Renzhi of Shanghai inspected education in various provinces and visited Longfu, inscribing the six characters "Dai Dongyuan Reading Place" on the lintel of the former site, which is extremely elegant. On the opposite bank is Taoli Garden, which covers over a thousand mu and produces peaches and plums with an annual value of several hundred thousand yuan. (2) About fifteen li from Tunxi, there is a town called Qianfu. Mr. Shi Hongyu, a Qing Dynasty scholar of Confucian classics, once lectured here. The opposite bank is Yashan Mountain, covered with green trees. Visitors who come here feel refreshed and relaxed. (3) About twenty li from Tunxi, there is Wansui Mountain, which is located on a cliff above a large river and is also known as Ancient City Rock. The mountain is full of rugged rocks. According to legend, it was where Zhu Taizu (the Hongwu Emperor) took refuge. Therefore, there is still a stone tablet with the three characters "Wansui Shan" standing majestically on the cliff overlooking the large river. It is also called Lianxin Stone. According to legend, Mr. Jin Zhengxi of the late Ming Dynasty would come here every morning. His feet would extend three-tenths of an inch outward to practice his mind. Some say that Jin Zhengxi's refusal to surrender to the Qing army was largely due to this practice. At the foot of the cliff, there are pavilions and towers, which are extremely exquisite. Since the Republic of China, it has been opened as a park. People sip tea there endlessly. To the east of the rock, there is a large stone bridge, which is over a hundred zhang long. The fourth station of the Xiutun Road is located here. (4) Five li outside the east gate of Xiuning City, which is twenty-five li from Tunxi, there is a town called Wan'an, which is the fifth station of the Xiutun Road. To the north is Xintang Village, where there is the Ginkgo Hall. Every beam and pillar of the hall is made of ginkgo wood. The current Anhui Second Middle School is built on the expansion of this hall. The town produces compasses, which are the best in the country. About 50% or 60% of the people are engaged in the compass industry.

▲Correction: In the article "Shandong Government Purchases 150 Long-Distance Buses" published in this journal on March 26, it was stated that the value was 300,000 yuan. It has now been verified that this is an error. This 300,000 yuan is the deposit paid for the first batch of 50 vehicles upon delivery and not the price for 150 vehicles. To avoid misunderstanding, we hereby solemnly declare a correction.

Letters 247

Reply to Mr. Wu Yinsheng's letter of April 12th

(1) Sir, according to the newspaper report yesterday, Mr. Wu Yinsheng is seeking a method to treat constipation. According to my teacher, Mr. Xie Liheng, people only know that constipation is a disease of the intestines and often use laxatives. Over time, the intestines become tired and ineffective. They do not know that this disease can be caused by the lungs not circulating qi, the stomach not descending qi, or the liver being congested with heat. It is appropriate to open the lungs, descend the stomach, or clear the liver. All of these can effectively relieve constipation. The so-called treatment of "separating two or three" in Chinese medicine is not like the Western medicine treatment of symptoms. Your condition includes dizziness, bad breath, and a yellow tongue coating, which indicates that stomach heat is steaming upward and cannot be cleared and descended. It is appropriate to use whole Trichosanthes fruit, immature bitter orange, Coptis chinensis, Pinellia ternata, and bamboo shavings. One or two doses can relieve constipation, and several more doses can reduce bad breath and yellow tongue coating. When the taste is right, the stomach heat will be removed, and the stool will naturally be lubricated. In addition, frequent walking can invigorate the peristaltic movement of the intestines, so that constipation will not occur often. Teacher Xie has served as president of various Chinese medicine schools and resides in Ningkang Lane on North Zhejiang Road. He has a long-standing reputation for treating diseases. You may wish to go and study with him. Sincerely, Wang Linfang.

(2) In reply, during my spare time from medical practice, I happened to read your letter in the newspaper describing your illness and suffering. As a doctor with a heart to save the world, I cannot but take it as my responsibility. I will now share my experience with you. The novelist Qin Shouou had constant constipation and pimples on his face. When he asked me for treatment, I said that it was due to damp heat in the stomach, which steamed between the muscles. I prescribed 0.5 fen of rhubarb powder in hot water every morning. After a month, his bowel movements were regular, and the pimples disappeared. Your condition is similar, so why not try it? According to the Materia Medica, rhubarb is bitter and cold, clears heat, and has the function of promoting the new and removing the old. Westerners often eat it as a tonic, which is reasonable. If it is ineffective, then the disease is slightly different. It is necessary to examine the physique and pulse before prescribing the right medicine. Sincerely, Chinese medicine practitioner Xie Yenong (Clinic: Lane 2, De'an Lane, west of the General Chamber of Commerce).

(3) Constipation is related to lifestyle and diseases of the stomach and intestines. Now that you have tried all kinds of laxatives without success, it is likely that the root cause has not been removed and your lifestyle has not been improved. If you send this letter to Dr. Zhang Senyu's clinic at No. 9 Maodeli, Zhangjia Bang, Meibai Road, he can indicate everything. Clinic hours are from 3:00 PM to 6:00 PM. I also enclose this information.

Science in superstition includes "Burning Tin Foil." Parenting includes "Starting Education from a Young Age." Marital life includes "Although My Face is Numb." Correspondence includes "How to Get a Job," etc. Novels include "Huangjia Village" by Tianxu, Wosheng, Xu Zhuodai, Yang'an, and Zhuming. It is sold in various newspaper stalls and cigarette shops in this city, and there are special distribution points in other cities, making it very convenient for readers. The price is 3 yuan per year, 1.6 yuan for half a year, and 0.3 yuan per copy. It is issued by the office of the Bureau at No. 15 Bowuyuan Road. The first issues in both Chinese and English have been published. The main items of the Chinese International Trade Guide are selected below: (1) The Purpose and Method of Export Commodity Inspection, (2) The Past Situation of Shanghai Cotton Inspection and the Inspection Status of the Bureau's Cotton Inspection Office, (3) Observing the History of Chinese Silk Trade from Statistics, (4) The Export Trade of Chinese Egg Products, (5) A Brief History of the Chinese Cotton Textile Industry, (6) Tung Oil Inspection Method, (7) Method of Identifying Silkworm Cocoons with Ackermann Ultraviolet Light Device, (8) Artificial Sausage Casings, (9) The Steps to be Taken by the Raw Silk Inspection Office. The sales outlets are the Commercial Press and the Beixin, Kaiming, Qixin, and Modern bookstores.

▲Luo Huizhu, a Cantonese prostitute from the Minxin Company, and Guo Jinhua, a former client, committed suicide by poison at the Dongya Hotel on March 24th due to their unsuccessful marriage plans, hoping to be united in the afterlife. Guo died immediately, and Luo passed away on the 7th of the month. It has been reported many times that Luo died for love. Before taking the poison, Luo was hired by the company to play the role of a famous prostitute in the film "Dreams of the Old Capital." A few days before taking the poison, she repeatedly urged the company to shoot the film first, claiming that she would be traveling far away. The company complied with her request because of her repeated urgings. Unexpectedly, the film was completed on March 24th, and the accident happened that evening. We must also fulfill our duties carefully in the present world. This is also (the image below is Luo's posthumous photo).

In the evening, they could hear the sound of drums and music as the villagers gathered to watch the company's actors rehearse stage plays. The work has now been completed, and over 9,000 feet of film have been shot, all of which are of excellent quality. The remaining indoor scenes are now being re-made, and the stage play is being rehearsed daily. The play will be performed soon.
